             setAiStageLoaded(false);\n   251‚Üí                setAiLoadError(null);\n   252‚Üí                setAiLoadAttempts(0);\n   253‚Üí                loadAiStageRunner();\n   254‚Üí              }}\n   255‚Üí              size=\"sm\"\n   256‚Üí            >\n   257‚Üí              Retry\n   258‚Üí            </Button>\n   259‚Üí          )\n   260‚Üí        });\n   261‚Üí      }\n   262‚Üí    }\n   263‚Üí  }, [toast, aiStageLoaded]);\n   264‚Üí\n   265‚Üí  // Load the AI stage runner dynamically with retries\n   266‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   267‚Üí    loadAiStageRunner();\n   268‚Üí  }, [loadAiStageRunner]);\n   269‚Üí\n   270‚Üí  // Auto-scroll utility\n   271‚Üí  const scrollToStageById = useCallback((stageId: string) => {\n   272‚Üí    const stageElement = 279‚Üí      });\n   280‚Üí    }\n   281‚Üí  }, []);\n   282‚Üí\n   283‚Üí  // Callback to sync instance changes from persistence layer\n   284‚Üí  const updateInstanceForPersistence = \n   290‚Üí    isSaving, \n   291‚Üí    lastSaved, \n   292‚Üí    saveError, \n   293‚Üí    documentId,\n   294‚Üí    saveDocument \n   295‚Üí  } = useDocumentPersistence({\n   296‚Üí    instance,\n   297‚Üí    updateInstance: updateInstanceForPersistence,\n   298‚Üí  });\n   299‚Üí\n   300‚Üí  const updateStageState = useCallback((stageId: string, updates: Partial<StageState>) => {\n   301‚Üí    let needsImmediateSave = false;\n   302‚Üí    const resultState = setInstance(prevInstance => {\n   303‚Üí      const newStageStates = {\n   304‚Üí        ...prevInstance.stageStates,\n   305‚Üí        [stageId]: {\n   306‚Üí          ...prevInstance.stageStates[stageId],\n   307‚Üí          ...updates,\n   308‚Üí        },\n   309‚Üí      };\n   310‚Üí      // Decide persistence before returning (so we can capture final merged state)\n   311‚Üí      if (prevInstance.stageStates[stageId]?.stageId === stageId) {\n   312‚Üí        const upd = updates as any;\n   313‚Üí        needsImmediateSave 321‚Üí\n   322‚Üí    if (needsImmediateSave) {\n   323‚Üí      // Next tick save so React state has committed\n   324‚Üí      setTimeout(() => {\n   325‚Üí        saveDocument();\n   326‚Üí      }, 0);\n   327‚Üí    }\n   328‚Üí  }, [saveDocument]);\n   329‚Üí\n   330‚Üí  // Enhanced dependency evaluation logic with support for autoRunConditions\n   331‚Üí  const evaluateDependenciesLogic = (currentStageStates: Record<string, StageState>, stages: Stage[]): Record<string, StageState> => {\n   332‚Üí    const newStageStates = { ...currentStageStates };\n   333‚Üí    let changed = false;\n   334‚Üí\n   335‚Üí    stages.forEach(stage => {\n   336‚Üí      const currentState = newStageStates[stage.id];\n   337‚Üí      if (!currentState) return; // Should not happen if initialized correctly\n   338‚Üí\n   339‚Üí      // Evaluate basic dependencies\n   340‚Üí      let depsMet = true;\n   341‚Üí      if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   342‚Üí        depsMet = stage.dependencies.every(depId => \n   343‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   344‚Üí        );\n   345‚Üí      }\n   346‚Üí\n   347‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun conditions (more complex dependency logic)\n   348‚Üí      let autoRunConditionsMet = true;\n   349‚Üí      if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   350‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll) {\n   351‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.every(depId => \n   352‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   353‚Üí          );\n   354‚Üí        }\n   355‚Üí        if (autoRunConditionsMet && stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny) {\n   356‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny.some(depId => \n   357‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   358‚Üí          );\n   359‚Üí        }\n   360‚Üí      }\n   361‚Üí      \n   362‚Üí      let isStale = false;\n   363‚Üí      if (currentState.status === 'completed' && currentState.output && currentState.completedAt) {\n   364‚Üí        // ONLY check staleness for truly completed stages\n   365‚Üí        const stageCompletedAt = new Date(currentState.completedAt).getTime();\n   366‚Üí        \n   367‚Üí        // Check staleness based on basic dependencies\n   368‚Üí        if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   369‚Üí          isStale = stage.dependencies.some(depId => {\n   370‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   371‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   372‚Üí          });\n   373‚Üí        }\n   374‚Üí        \n   375‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun conditions\n   376‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autoRunConditions?.requiresAll) {\n   377‚Üí          isStale = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.some(depId => {\n   378‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   379‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   380‚Üí          });\n   381‚Üí        }\n   382‚Üí        \n   383‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun dependencies\n   384‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   385‚Üí          isStale = stage.autorunDependsOn.some(depId => {\n   386‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   387‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   388‚Üí          });\n   389‚Üí        }\n   390‚Üí      }\n   391‚Üí\n   392‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun dependencies (separate from activation dependencies)\n   393‚Üí      let autorunDepsMet = true;\n   394‚Üí      if (stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   395‚Üí        // Use explicit autorun dependencies\n   396‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = stage.autorunDependsOn.every(depId => \n   397‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   398‚Üí        );\n   399‚Üí      } else {\n   400‚Üí        // Fall back to regular dependencies (backward compatibility)\n   401‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = depsMet;\n   402‚Üí      }\n   403‚Üí\n   404‚Üí      // Determine if stage should auto-run\n   405‚Üí      let shouldAutoRun = false;\n   406‚Üí      if (stage.autoRun && currentState.status === 'idle' && !currentState.isEditingOutput) {\n   407‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   408‚Üí          // Use complex autorun conditions AND autorun dependencies\n   409‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autoRunConditionsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   410‚Üí        } else {\n   411‚Üí          // Use simple dependency logic - stage must be active (depsMet) AND autorun deps met\n   412‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   413‚Üí        }\n   414‚Üí      }\n   415‚Üí\n   416‚Üí      if (\n   417‚Üí        currentState.depsAreMet !== depsMet ||\n   418‚Üí        currentState.isStale !== isStale ||\n   419‚Üí        currentState.shouldAutoRun !== shouldAutoRun\n   420‚Üí      ) {\n   421‚Üí        newStageStates[stage.id] = {\n   422‚Üí          ...currentState,\n   423‚Üí          depsAreMet: depsMet,\n   424‚Üí          isStale: isStale,\n   425‚Üí          shouldAutoRun: shouldAutoRun,\n   426‚Üí          // Reset staleDismissed when stage is no longer stale\n   427‚Üí          staleDismissed: isStale ? currentState.staleDismissed : false,\n   428‚Üí        };\n   429‚Üí        changed = true;\n   430‚Üí      }\n   431‚Üí    });\n   432‚Üí    return changed ? newStageStates : currentStageStates; // Return original if no change to avoid re-render\n   433‚Üí  };\n   434‚Üí  \n   435‚Üí  // Effect for initial and subsequent dependency evaluations\n   436‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   437‚Üí    setInstance(prevInstance => ({\n   438‚Üí      ...prevInstance,\n   439‚Üí      stageStates: evaluateDependenciesLogic(prevInstance.stageStates, prevInstance.workflow.stages)\n   440‚Üí    }));\n   441‚Üí  }, []); // Runs once on mount, subsequent calls via updateStageState\n   442‚Üí\n   443‚Üí\n   444‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   445‚Üí    instance.workflow.stages.forEach(stage => {\n   446‚Üí      const stageState = instance.stageStates[stage.id];\n   447‚Üí      // Defensive check: ensure stageState exists before accessing its properties\n   448‚Üí      if (stageState && }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.stages]); \n   455‚Üí\n   456‚Üí\n   457‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   458‚Üí    const titleStageId = instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput;\n   459‚Üí    if (titleStageId) {\n   460‚Üí      const titleStageState = instance.stageStates[titleStageId];\n   461‚Üí      if (titleStageState?.status === 'completed' && titleStageState.output) {\n 495‚Üí\n   496‚Üí\n   497‚Üí  const handleInputChange = (stageId: string, fieldName: string, value: any) => {\n   498‚Üí    // This is primarily for simple input types like 'textarea' or 'context' (stageId: string, currentInput?: any, aiRedoNotes?: string) => {\n   532‚Üí    const stage = instance.workflow.stages.find(s => s.id === stageId);\n   533‚Üí    const stageTitle = stage?.title || aiLoadAttempts,\n   544‚Üí      timeSinceLoadMs: timeSinceLoad,\n   545‚Üí      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n   546‚Üí    });\n   547‚Üí    \n   548‚Üí    if (!aiStageLoaded || !runAiStage) 554‚Üí        timeSinceLoadMs: timeSinceLoad,\n   555‚Üí        networkOnline: navigator.onLine,\n   556‚Üí        connectionType: (navigator as any).connection?.effectiveType || 'unknown',\n   557‚Üí     errorTitle = \"AI Module Failed to Load\";\n   572‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system encountered an error during initialization and cannot process \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   573‚Üí </Button>\n   641‚Üí        )\n   642‚Üí      });\n   643‚Üí      \n   644‚Üí      return;\n   645‚Üí    }\n   646‚Üí\n   647‚Üí    console.log('[handleRunStage] ‚úÖ AI system ready, proceeding with dependencies and autorun conditions.\n   438‚Üí   * It processes all stages in the workflow and updates their readiness status.\n   439‚Üí   * \n   440‚Üí   * @param currentStageStates - Current state of all workflow stages\n   441‚Üí   * @param stages - Array of stage definitions from the workflow\n   442‚Üí   * @returns Updated stage states with dependency and autorun evaluation results\n   443‚Üí   * \n   444‚Üí   * Key functionality:\n   445‚Üí   * - Evaluates basic dependencies (dependsOn relationships)\n   446‚Üí   * - Processes autorun conditions with configurable logic\n   447‚Üí   * - Handles complex dependency chains and circular dependency detection\n   448‚Üí   * - Automatically marks stages as ready when dependencies are met\n   449‚Üí   * - Manages autorun flags for stages that should execute immediately\n   450‚Üí   * \n   451‚Üí   * Autorun conditions supported:\n   452‚Üí   * - 'always': Always autorun when dependencies are met\n   453‚Üí   * - 'never': Never autorun, requires manual execution\n   454‚Üí   * - 'conditional': Autorun based on custom logic\n   455‚Üí   * \n   456‚Üí   * @example\n   457‚Üí   * ```typescript\n   458‚Üí   * const evaluatedStates = evaluateDependenciesLogic(stageStates, workflowStages);\n   459‚Üí   * ```\n   460‚Üí   */\n   461‚Üí  const evaluateDependenciesLogic = (currentStageStates: Record<string, StageState>, stages: Stage[]): Record<string, StageState> => {\n   462‚Üí    const newStageStates = { ...currentStageStates };\n   463‚Üí    let changed = false;\n   464‚Üí\n   465‚Üí    stages.forEach(stage => {\n   466‚Üí      const currentState = newStageStates[stage.id];\n   467‚Üí      if (!currentState) return; // Should not happen if initialized correctly\n   468‚Üí\n   469‚Üí      // Evaluate basic dependencies\n   470‚Üí      let depsMet = true;\n   471‚Üí      if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   472‚Üí        depsMet = stage.dependencies.every(depId => \n   473‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   474‚Üí        );\n   475‚Üí      }\n   476‚Üí\n   477‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun conditions (more complex dependency logic)\n   478‚Üí      let autoRunConditionsMet = true;\n   479‚Üí      if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   480‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll) {\n   481‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.every(depId => \n   482‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   483‚Üí          );\n   484‚Üí        }\n   485‚Üí        if (autoRunConditionsMet && stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny) {\n   486‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny.some(depId => \n   487‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   488‚Üí          );\n   489‚Üí        }\n   490‚Üí      }\n   491‚Üí      \n   492‚Üí      let isStale = false;\n   493‚Üí      if (currentState.status === 'completed' && currentState.output && currentState.completedAt) {\n   494‚Üí        // ONLY check staleness for truly completed stages\n   495‚Üí        const stageCompletedAt = new Date(currentState.completedAt).getTime();\n   496‚Üí        \n   497‚Üí        // Check staleness based on basic dependencies\n   498‚Üí        if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   499‚Üí          isStale = stage.dependencies.some(depId => {\n   500‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   501‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   502‚Üí          });\n   503‚Üí        }\n   504‚Üí        \n   505‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun conditions\n   506‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autoRunConditions?.requiresAll) {\n   507‚Üí          isStale = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.some(depId => {\n   508‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   509‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   510‚Üí          });\n   511‚Üí        }\n   512‚Üí        \n   513‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun dependencies\n   514‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   515‚Üí          isStale = stage.autorunDependsOn.some(depId => {\n   516‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   517‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   518‚Üí          });\n   519‚Üí        }\n   520‚Üí      }\n   521‚Üí\n   522‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun dependencies (separate from activation dependencies)\n   523‚Üí      let autorunDepsMet = true;\n   524‚Üí      if (stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   525‚Üí        // Use explicit autorun dependencies\n   526‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = stage.autorunDependsOn.every(depId => \n   527‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   528‚Üí        );\n   529‚Üí      } else {\n   530‚Üí        // Fall back to regular dependencies (backward compatibility)\n   531‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = depsMet;\n   532‚Üí      }\n   533‚Üí\n   534‚Üí      // Determine if stage should auto-run\n   535‚Üí      let shouldAutoRun = false;\n   536‚Üí      if (stage.autoRun && currentState.status === 'idle' && !currentState.isEditingOutput) {\n   537‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   538‚Üí          // Use complex autorun conditions AND autorun dependencies\n   539‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autoRunConditionsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   540‚Üí        } else {\n   541‚Üí          // Use simple dependency logic - stage must be active (depsMet) AND autorun deps met\n   542‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   543‚Üí        }\n   544‚Üí      }\n   545‚Üí\n   546‚Üí      if (\n   547‚Üí        currentState.depsAreMet !== depsMet ||\n   548‚Üí        currentState.isStale !== isStale ||\n   549‚Üí        currentState.shouldAutoRun !== shouldAutoRun\n   550‚Üí      ) {\n   551‚Üí        newStageStates[stage.id] = {\n   552‚Üí          ...currentState,\n   553‚Üí          depsAreMet: depsMet,\n   554‚Üí          isStale: isStale,\n   555‚Üí          shouldAutoRun: shouldAutoRun,\n   556‚Üí          // Reset staleDismissed when stage is no longer stale\n   557‚Üí          staleDismissed: isStale ? currentState.staleDismissed : false,\n   558‚Üí        };\n   559‚Üí        changed = true;\n   560‚Üí      }\n   561‚Üí    });\n   562‚Üí    return changed ? newStageStates : currentStageStates; // Return original if no change to avoid re-render\n   563‚Üí  };\n   564‚Üí  \n   565‚Üí  // Effect for initial and subsequent dependency evaluations\n   566‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   567‚Üí    setInstance(prevInstance => ({\n   568‚Üí      ...prevInstance,\n   569‚Üí      stageStates: evaluateDependenciesLogic(prevInstance.stageStates, prevInstance.workflow.stages)\n   570‚Üí    }));\n   571‚Üí  }, []); // Runs once on mount, subsequent calls via updateStageState\n   572‚Üí\n   573‚Üí\n   574‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   575‚Üí    instance.workflow.stages.forEach(stage => {\n   576‚Üí      const stageState = instance.stageStates[stage.id];\n   577‚Üí      // Defensive check: ensure stageState exists before accessing its properties\n   578‚Üí      if (stageState && stageState.shouldAutoRun && stageState.status === 'idle' && stageState.depsAreMet && !stageState.isEditingOutput) {\n   579‚Üí        console.log(`[Autorun] Triggering autorun for stage ${stage.id}`);\n   580‚Üí        handleRunStage(stage.id, stageState.userInput);\n   581‚Üí      }\n   582‚Üí    });\n   583‚Üí    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps\n   584‚Üí  }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.stages]); \n   585‚Üí\n   586‚Üí\n   587‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   588‚Üí    const titleStageId = instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput;\n   589‚Üí    if (titleStageId) {\n   590‚Üí      const titleStageState = instance.stageStates[titleStageId];\n   591‚Üí      if (titleStageState?.status === 'completed' && titleStageState.output) {\n   592‚Üí        let newTitle = \"\";\n   593‚Üí        if (typeof titleStageState.output === 'string') {\n   594‚Üí            newTitle = titleStageState.output;\n   595‚Üí        } \n   596‚Üí        else if (titleStageId === \"page-title-generation\" && typeof titleStageState.output === 'object' && titleStageState.output !== null && Array.isArray(titleStageState.output.titles) && titleStageState.output.titles.length > 0) {\n   597‚Üí            // For page-title-generation, if 'chosenTitle' exists in outline-creation's userInput, use that.\n   598‚Üí            const outlineStageUserInput = instance.stageStates['outline-creation']?.userInput;\n   599‚Üí            if (outlineStageUserInput && typeof outlineStageUserInput === 'object' && outlineStageUserInput.chosenTitle) {\n   600‚Üí                 newTitle = outlineStageUserInput.chosenTitle;\n   601‚Üí            } else {\n   602‚Üí                newTitle = titleStageState.output.titles[0]; \n   603‚Üí            }\n   604‚Üí        }\n   605‚Üí         else if (titleStageId === \"dish-name\" && typeof titleStageState.output === 'string') { // For Recipe Workflow\n   606‚Üí            newTitle = titleStageState.output;\n   607‚Üí        }\n   608‚Üí        else if (typeof titleStageState.output === 'object' && titleStageState.output !== null && titleStageState.output.title) { // Generic title from object\n   609‚Üí             newTitle = titleStageState.output.title;\n   610‚Üí        }\n   611‚Üí        \n   612‚Üí        if (newTitle && newTitle.length > 0 && newTitle.length < 150) { \n   613‚Üí            setPageTitle(newTitle);\n   614‚Üí            if (typeof document !== 'undefined') {\n   615‚Üí                document.title = `${newTitle} - ${siteConfig.name}`;\n   616‚Üí            }\n   617‚Üí            setInstance(prev => ({\n   618‚Üí                ...prev,\n   619‚Üí                document: { ...prev.document, title: newTitle }\n   620‚Üí            }));\n   621‚Üí        }\n   622‚Üí      }\n   623‚Üí    }\n   624‚Üí  }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput]);\n   625‚Üí\n   626‚Üí\n   627‚Üí  const handleInputChange = (stageId: string, fieldName: string, value: any) => {\n   628‚Üí    // This is primarily for simple input types like 'textarea' or 'context' === stageId);\n   639‚Üí    if (!stage) return;\n   640‚Üí\n   641‚Üí    // For form stages without a promptTemplate, immediately mark as completed with the form data as output\n   642‚Üí    if (stageId: string, currentInput?: any, aiRedoNotes?: string) => {\n   662‚Üí    const stage = instance.workflow.stages.find(s => s.id === stageId);\n   663‚Üí    const stageTitle = stage?.title || stageId;\n   664‚Üí    const currentTime = Date.now();\n   665‚Üí    const timeSinceLoad = currentTime - aiLoadStartTime;\n   666‚Üí    \n   667‚Üí    console.log('[handleRunStage] AI readiness aiLoadAttempts,\n   674‚Üí      timeSinceLoadMs: timeSinceLoad,\n   675‚Üí      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n   676‚Üí    });\n   677‚Üí    \n   678‚Üí    if (!aiStageLoaded || !runAiStage) {\n   679‚Üí      const diagnosticInfo = {\n   680‚Üí        aiStageLoaded,\n   681‚Üí        runAiStageExists: !!runAiStage,\n   682‚Üí        aiLoadError,\n   683‚Üí        aiLoadAttempts,\n   684‚Üí        timeSinceLoadMs: timeSinceLoad,\n   685‚Üí        networkOnline: navigator.onLine,\n   686‚Üí        connectionType: (navigator as any).connection?.effectiveType || 'unknown',\n   687‚Üí        userAgent: navigator.userAgent,\n   688‚Üí        url: window.location.href,\n   689‚Üí        stageId,\n   690‚Üí        stageTitle,\n   691‚Üí      };\n   692‚Üí      \n   693‚Üí errorTitle = \"AI System Not Ready\";\n   697‚Üí      let errorDescription = \"\";\n   698‚Üí      let actionableSteps: string[] = [];\n   699‚Üí      \n   700‚Üí      if (aiLoadError) {\n   701‚Üí        errorTitle = \"AI Module Failed to Load\";\n   702‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system encountered an error during initialization and cannot process \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   703‚Üí < 10000) {\n   711‚Üí        errorTitle = \"AI System Still Loading\";\n   712‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system is still initializing. Please wait a moment before running \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   713‚Üí        actionableSteps = [\n   714‚Üí          `Wait ${Math.ceil((10000 - timeSinceLoad) / 1000)} more seconds`,\n   715‚Üí          \"Try again in a few seconds\",\n   716‚Üí          \"Ensure stable internet connection\",\n   717‚Üí          \"Try refreshing if loading takes too long\"\n   718‚Üí        ];\n   719‚Üí      } else {\n   720‚Üí        errorTitle = \"AI System Load Timeout\";\n   721‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system failed to load after ${Math.round(timeSinceLoad / 1000)} seconds. </Button>\n   771‚Üí        )\n   772‚Üí      });\n   773‚Üí      \n   774‚Üí      return;\n   775‚Üí    }\n   776‚Üí\n   777‚Üí    console.log('[handleRunStage] ‚úÖ AI system ready, proceeding with 812‚Üí      try {\n   813‚Üí        const { executeExportStage } = await import('@/ai/flows/export-stage-execution');\n   814‚Üí        \n   815‚Üí        console.log('[handleRunStage] 443‚Üí   * \n   444‚Üí   * Key functionality:\n   445‚Üí   * - Evaluates basic dependencies (dependsOn relationships)\n   446‚Üí   * - Processes autorun conditions with configurable logic\n   447‚Üí   * - Handles complex dependency chains and circular dependency detection\n   448‚Üí   * - Automatically marks stages as ready when dependencies are met\n   449‚Üí   * - Manages autorun flags for stages that should execute immediately\n   450‚Üí   * \n   451‚Üí   * Autorun conditions supported:\n   452‚Üí   * - 'always': Always autorun when dependencies are met\n   453‚Üí   * - 'never': Never autorun, requires manual execution\n   454‚Üí   * - 'conditional': Autorun based on custom logic\n   455‚Üí   * \n   456‚Üí   * @example\n   457‚Üí   * ```typescript\n   458‚Üí   * const evaluatedStates = evaluateDependenciesLogic(stageStates, workflowStages);\n   459‚Üí   * ```\n   460‚Üí   */\n   461‚Üí  const evaluateDependenciesLogic = (currentStageStates: Record<string, StageState>, stages: Stage[]): Record<string, StageState> => {\n   462‚Üí    const newStageStates = { ...currentStageStates };\n   463‚Üí    let changed = false;\n   464‚Üí\n   465‚Üí    stages.forEach(stage => {\n   466‚Üí      const currentState = newStageStates[stage.id];\n   467‚Üí      if (!currentState) return; // Should not happen if initialized correctly\n   468‚Üí\n   469‚Üí      // Evaluate basic dependencies\n   470‚Üí      let depsMet = true;\n   471‚Üí      if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   472‚Üí        depsMet = stage.dependencies.every(depId => \n   473‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   474‚Üí        );\n   475‚Üí      }\n   476‚Üí\n   477‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun conditions (more complex dependency logic)\n   478‚Üí      let autoRunConditionsMet = true;\n   479‚Üí      if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   480‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll) {\n   481‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.every(depId => \n   482‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   483‚Üí          );\n   484‚Üí        }\n   485‚Üí        if (autoRunConditionsMet && stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny) {\n   486‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny.some(depId => \n   487‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   488‚Üí          );\n   489‚Üí        }\n   490‚Üí      }\n   491‚Üí      \n   492‚Üí      let isStale = false;\n   493‚Üí      if (currentState.status === 'completed' && currentState.output && currentState.completedAt) {\n   494‚Üí        // ONLY check staleness for truly completed stages\n   495‚Üí        const stageCompletedAt = new Date(currentState.completedAt).getTime();\n   496‚Üí        \n   497‚Üí        // Check staleness based on basic dependencies\n   498‚Üí        if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   499‚Üí          isStale = stage.dependencies.some(depId => {\n   500‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   501‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   502‚Üí          });\n   503‚Üí        }\n   504‚Üí        \n   505‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun conditions\n   506‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autoRunConditions?.requiresAll) {\n   507‚Üí          isStale = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.some(depId => {\n   508‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   509‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   510‚Üí          });\n   511‚Üí        }\n   512‚Üí        \n   513‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun dependencies\n   514‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   515‚Üí          isStale = stage.autorunDependsOn.some(depId => {\n   516‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   517‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   518‚Üí          });\n   519‚Üí        }\n   520‚Üí      }\n   521‚Üí\n   522‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun dependencies (separate from activation dependencies)\n   523‚Üí      let autorunDepsMet = true;\n   524‚Üí      if (stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   525‚Üí        // Use explicit autorun dependencies\n   526‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = stage.autorunDependsOn.every(depId => \n   527‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   528‚Üí        );\n   529‚Üí      } else {\n   530‚Üí        // Fall back to regular dependencies (backward compatibility)\n   531‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = depsMet;\n   532‚Üí      }\n   533‚Üí\n   534‚Üí      // Determine if stage should auto-run\n   535‚Üí      let shouldAutoRun = false;\n   536‚Üí      if (stage.autoRun && currentState.status === 'idle' && !currentState.isEditingOutput) {\n   537‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   538‚Üí          // Use complex autorun conditions AND autorun dependencies\n   539‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autoRunConditionsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   540‚Üí        } else {\n   541‚Üí          // Use simple dependency logic - stage must be active (depsMet) AND autorun deps met\n   542‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   543‚Üí        }\n   544‚Üí      }\n   545‚Üí\n   546‚Üí      if (\n   547‚Üí        currentState.depsAreMet !== depsMet ||\n   548‚Üí        currentState.isStale !== isStale ||\n   549‚Üí        currentState.shouldAutoRun !== shouldAutoRun\n   550‚Üí      ) {\n   551‚Üí        newStageStates[stage.id] = {\n   552‚Üí          ...currentState,\n   553‚Üí          depsAreMet: depsMet,\n   554‚Üí          isStale: isStale,\n   555‚Üí          shouldAutoRun: shouldAutoRun,\n   556‚Üí          // Reset staleDismissed when stage is no longer stale\n   557‚Üí          staleDismissed: isStale ? currentState.staleDismissed : false,\n   558‚Üí        };\n   559‚Üí        changed = true;\n   560‚Üí      }\n   561‚Üí    });\n   562‚Üí    return changed ? newStageStates : currentStageStates; // Return original if no change to avoid re-render\n   563‚Üí  };\n   564‚Üí  \n   565‚Üí  // Effect for initial and subsequent dependency evaluations\n   566‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   567‚Üí    setInstance(prevInstance => ({\n   568‚Üí      ...prevInstance,\n   569‚Üí      stageStates: evaluateDependenciesLogic(prevInstance.stageStates, prevInstance.workflow.stages)\n   570‚Üí    }));\n   571‚Üí  }, []); // Runs once on mount, subsequent calls via updateStageState\n   572‚Üí\n   573‚Üí\n   574‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   575‚Üí    instance.workflow.stages.forEach(stage => {\n   576‚Üí      const stageState = instance.stageStates[stage.id];\n   577‚Üí      // Defensive check: ensure stageState exists before accessing its properties\n   578‚Üí      if (stageState && stageState.shouldAutoRun && stageState.status === 'idle' && stageState.depsAreMet && !stageState.isEditingOutput) {\n   579‚Üí        console.log(`[Autorun] Triggering autorun for stage ${stage.id}`);\n   580‚Üí        handleRunStage(stage.id, stageState.userInput);\n   581‚Üí      }\n   582‚Üí    });\n   583‚Üí    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps\n   584‚Üí  }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.stages]); \n   585‚Üí\n   586‚Üí\n   587‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   588‚Üí    const titleStageId = instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput;\n   589‚Üí    if (titleStageId) {\n   590‚Üí      const titleStageState = instance.stageStates[titleStageId];\n   591‚Üí      if (titleStageState?.status === 'completed' && titleStageState.output) {\n   592‚Üí        let newTitle = \"\";\n   593‚Üí        if (typeof titleStageState.output === 'string') {\n   594‚Üí            newTitle = titleStageState.output;\n   595‚Üí        } \n   596‚Üí outlineStageUserInput.chosenTitle) {\n   600‚Üí                 newTitle = outlineStageUserInput.chosenTitle;\n   601‚Üí            } else {\n   602‚Üí                newTitle = titleStageState.output.titles[0]; \n   603‚Üí            }\n   604‚Üí        }\n   605‚Üí         else if (titleStageId === \"dish-name\" && typeof titleStageState.output === 'string') { // For Recipe 625‚Üí\n   626‚Üí\n   627‚Üí  const handleInputChange = (stageId: string, fieldName: string, value: any) => {\n   628‚Üí    // This is primarily for simple input types like 'textarea' or 'context' stage with comprehensive error handling and AI system integration\n   663‚Üí   * \n   664‚Üí   * This is the core stage execution function that handles both AI-powered stages and\n   665‚Üí   * non-AI stages (like export stages). It manages the complete execution lifecycle\n   666‚Üí   * including input validation, AI system readiness checks, error handling, and\n   667‚Üí   * state management.\n   668‚Üí   * \n   669‚Üí   * @param stageId - Unique identifier of the stage to execute\n   670‚Üí   * @param currentInput - Optional input data for the stage (overrides stage state)\n   671‚Üí   * @param aiRedoNotes - Optional notes for AI regeneration requests\n   672‚Üí   * @returns Promise that resolves when stage execution completes\n   673‚Üí   * \n   674‚Üí   * Stage execution process:\n   675‚Üí   * 1. **Pre-execution validation**: Checks AI system readiness and stage configuration\n   676‚Üí   * 2. **Input preparation**: Resolves template variables and prepares stage input\n   677‚Üí   * 3. **Execution routing**: Routes to appropriate handler (AI vs non-AI stages)\n   678‚Üí   * 4. **Result processing**: Validates and processes stage output\n   679‚Üí   * 5. **State management**: Updates stage state and triggers dependency evaluation\n   680‚Üí   * 6. **Error handling**: Comprehensive error catching and user feedback\n   681‚Üí   * \n   682‚Üí   * Special stage types:\n   683‚Üí   * - **AI stages**: Executed via AI stage runner with model-specific handling\n   684‚Üí   * - **Export stages**: Handled by specialized export stage execution\n   685‚Üí   * - **Form stages**: Process form data and trigger dependent stages\n   686‚Üí   * - **Template stages**: Resolve template variables from workflow context\n   687‚Üí   * \n   688‚Üí   * Error handling:\n   689‚Üí   * - AI system not ready errors with actionable solutions\n   690‚Üí   * - Please wait a moment before running \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   755‚Üí        actionableSteps = [\n   756‚Üí          `Wait ${Math.ceil((10000 - timeSinceLoad) / 1000)} more seconds`,\n   757‚Üí          \"Try again in a few seconds\",\n   758‚Üí          \"Ensure stable internet connection\",\n   759‚Üí          \"Try refreshing if loading takes too long\"\n   760‚Üí        ];\n   761‚Üí      } else {\n   762‚Üí        errorTitle = \"AI System Load Timeout\";\n   763‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system failed to load after ${Math.round(timeSinceLoad / 1000)} seconds. Cannot process \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   764‚Üí        actionableSteps = [\n   765‚Üí          \"Refresh the page (most likely to fix)\",\n   766‚Üí          \"Clear browser cache and cookies\",\n   767‚Üí          \"Check your internet connection speed\",\n   768‚Üí          \"Open browser console to see detailed errors\",\n   769‚Üí          \"Try a different browser or incognito mode\"\n   770‚Üí        ];\n   771‚Üí      }\n   772‚Üí      \n   773‚Üí      const detailedError = `${errorDescription}\n   774‚Üí\n   775‚ÜíTechnical Status:\n   776‚Üí‚Ä¢ AI Module Loaded: ${aiStageLoaded ? </Button>\n   813‚Üí        )\n   814‚Üí      });\n   815‚Üí      \n   816‚Üí      return;\n   817‚Üí    }\n   818‚Üí\n   819‚Üí    console.log('[handleRunStage] ‚úÖ AI system ready, proceeding with 443‚Üí   * \n   444‚Üí   * Key functionality:\n   445‚Üí   * - Evaluates basic dependencies (dependsOn relationships)\n   446‚Üí   * - Processes autorun conditions with configurable logic\n   447‚Üí   * - Handles complex dependency chains and circular dependency detection\n   448‚Üí   * - Automatically marks stages as ready when dependencies are met\n   449‚Üí   * - Manages autorun flags for stages that should execute immediately\n   450‚Üí   * \n   451‚Üí   * Autorun conditions supported:\n   452‚Üí   * - 'always': Always autorun when dependencies are met\n   453‚Üí   * - 'never': Never autorun, requires manual execution\n   454‚Üí   * - 'conditional': Autorun based on custom logic\n   455‚Üí   * \n   456‚Üí   * @example\n   457‚Üí   * ```typescript\n   458‚Üí   * const evaluatedStates = evaluateDependenciesLogic(stageStates, workflowStages);\n   459‚Üí   * ```\n   460‚Üí   */\n   461‚Üí  const evaluateDependenciesLogic = (currentStageStates: Record<string, StageState>, stages: Stage[]): Record<string, StageState> => {\n   462‚Üí    const newStageStates = { ...currentStageStates };\n   463‚Üí    let changed = false;\n   464‚Üí\n   465‚Üí    stages.forEach(stage => {\n   466‚Üí      const currentState = newStageStates[stage.id];\n   467‚Üí      if (!currentState) return; // Should not happen if initialized correctly\n   468‚Üí\n   469‚Üí      // Evaluate basic dependencies\n   470‚Üí      let depsMet = true;\n   471‚Üí      if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   472‚Üí        depsMet = stage.dependencies.every(depId => \n   473‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   474‚Üí        );\n   475‚Üí      }\n   476‚Üí\n   477‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun conditions (more complex dependency logic)\n   478‚Üí      let autoRunConditionsMet = true;\n   479‚Üí      if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   480‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll) {\n   481‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.every(depId => \n   482‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   483‚Üí          );\n   484‚Üí        }\n   485‚Üí        if (autoRunConditionsMet && stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny) {\n   486‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny.some(depId => \n   487‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   488‚Üí          );\n   489‚Üí        }\n   490‚Üí      }\n   491‚Üí      \n   492‚Üí      let isStale = false;\n   493‚Üí      if (currentState.status === 'completed' && currentState.output && currentState.completedAt) {\n   494‚Üí        // ONLY check staleness for truly completed stages\n   495‚Üí        const stageCompletedAt = new Date(currentState.completedAt).getTime();\n   496‚Üí        \n   497‚Üí        // Check staleness based on basic dependencies\n   498‚Üí        if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   499‚Üí          isStale = stage.dependencies.some(depId => {\n   500‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   501‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   502‚Üí          });\n   503‚Üí        }\n   504‚Üí        \n   505‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun conditions\n   506‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autoRunConditions?.requiresAll) {\n   507‚Üí          isStale = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.some(depId => {\n   508‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   509‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   510‚Üí          });\n   511‚Üí        }\n   512‚Üí        \n   513‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun dependencies\n   514‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   515‚Üí          isStale = stage.autorunDependsOn.some(depId => {\n   516‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   517‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   518‚Üí          });\n   519‚Üí        }\n   520‚Üí      }\n   521‚Üí\n   522‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun dependencies (separate from activation dependencies)\n   523‚Üí      let autorunDepsMet = true;\n   524‚Üí      if (stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   525‚Üí        // Use explicit autorun dependencies\n   526‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = stage.autorunDependsOn.every(depId => \n   527‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   528‚Üí        );\n   529‚Üí      } else {\n   530‚Üí        // Fall back to regular dependencies (backward compatibility)\n   531‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = depsMet;\n   532‚Üí      }\n   533‚Üí\n   534‚Üí      // Determine if stage should auto-run\n   535‚Üí      let shouldAutoRun = false;\n   536‚Üí      if (stage.autoRun && currentState.status === 'idle' && !currentState.isEditingOutput) {\n   537‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   538‚Üí          // Use complex autorun conditions AND autorun dependencies\n   539‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autoRunConditionsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   540‚Üí        } else {\n   541‚Üí          // Use simple dependency logic - stage must be active (depsMet) AND autorun deps met\n   542‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   543‚Üí        }\n   544‚Üí      }\n   545‚Üí\n   546‚Üí      if (\n   547‚Üí        currentState.depsAreMet !== depsMet ||\n   548‚Üí        currentState.isStale !== isStale ||\n   549‚Üí        currentState.shouldAutoRun !== shouldAutoRun\n   550‚Üí      ) {\n   551‚Üí        newStageStates[stage.id] = {\n   552‚Üí          ...currentState,\n   553‚Üí          depsAreMet: depsMet,\n   554‚Üí          isStale: isStale,\n   555‚Üí          shouldAutoRun: shouldAutoRun,\n   556‚Üí          // Reset staleDismissed when stage is no longer stale\n   557‚Üí          staleDismissed: isStale ? currentState.staleDismissed : false,\n   558‚Üí        };\n   559‚Üí        changed = true;\n   560‚Üí      }\n   561‚Üí    });\n   562‚Üí    return changed ? newStageStates : currentStageStates; // Return original if no change to avoid re-render\n   563‚Üí  };\n   564‚Üí  \n   565‚Üí  // Effect for initial and subsequent dependency evaluations\n   566‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   567‚Üí    setInstance(prevInstance => ({\n   568‚Üí      ...prevInstance,\n   569‚Üí      stageStates: evaluateDependenciesLogic(prevInstance.stageStates, prevInstance.workflow.stages)\n   570‚Üí    }));\n   571‚Üí  }, []); // Runs once on mount, subsequent calls via updateStageState\n   572‚Üí\n   573‚Üí\n   574‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   575‚Üí    instance.workflow.stages.forEach(stage => {\n   576‚Üí      const stageState = instance.stageStates[stage.id];\n   577‚Üí      // Defensive check: ensure stageState exists before accessing its properties\n   578‚Üí      if (stageState && stageState.shouldAutoRun && stageState.status === 'idle' && stageState.depsAreMet && !stageState.isEditingOutput) {\n   579‚Üí        console.log(`[Autorun] Triggering autorun for stage ${stage.id}`);\n   580‚Üí        handleRunStage(stage.id, stageState.userInput);\n   581‚Üí      }\n   582‚Üí    });\n   583‚Üí    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps\n   584‚Üí  }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.stages]); \n   585‚Üí\n   586‚Üí\n   587‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   588‚Üí    const titleStageId = instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput;\n   589‚Üí    if (titleStageId) {\n   590‚Üí      const titleStageState = instance.stageStates[titleStageId];\n   591‚Üí      if (titleStageState?.status === 'completed' && titleStageState.output) {\n   592‚Üí        let newTitle = \"\";\n   593‚Üí        if (typeof titleStageState.output === 'string') {\n   594‚Üí            newTitle = titleStageState.output;\n   595‚Üí        } \n   596‚Üí        else if (titleStageId === \"page-title-generation\" && typeof titleStageState.output === 'object' && titleStageState.output !== null && Array.isArray(titleStageState.output.titles) && titleStageState.output.titles.length > 0) {\n   597‚Üí            // For page-title-generation, if 'chosenTitle' exists in outline-creation's userInput, use that.\n   598‚Üí            const outlineStageUserInput = instance.stageStates['outline-creation']?.userInput;\n   599‚Üí            if (outlineStageUserInput && typeof outlineStageUserInput === 'object' && outlineStageUserInput.chosenTitle) {\n   600‚Üí                 newTitle = outlineStageUserInput.chosenTitle;\n   601‚Üí            } else {\n   602‚Üí                newTitle = titleStageState.output.titles[0]; \n   603‚Üí            }\n   604‚Üí        }\n   605‚Üí         else if (titleStageId === \"dish-name\" && typeof titleStageState.output === 'string') { // For Recipe Workflow\n   606‚Üí            newTitle = titleStageState.output;\n   607‚Üí        }\n   608‚Üí        else if (typeof titleStageState.output === 'object' && titleStageState.output !== null && titleStageState.output.title) { // Generic title from object\n   609‚Üí             newTitle = titleStageState.output.title;\n   610‚Üí        }\n   611‚Üí        \n   612‚Üí        if (newTitle && newTitle.length > 0 && newTitle.length < 150) { \n   613‚Üí            setPageTitle(newTitle);\n   614‚Üí            if (typeof document !== 'undefined') {\n   615‚Üí                document.title = `${newTitle} - ${siteConfig.name}`;\n   616‚Üí            }\n   617‚Üí            setInstance(prev => ({\n   618‚Üí                ...prev,\n   619‚Üí                document: { ...prev.document, title: newTitle }\n   620‚Üí            }));\n   621‚Üí        }\n   622‚Üí      }\n   623‚Üí    }\n   624‚Üí  }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput]);\n   625‚Üí\n   626‚Üí\n   627‚Üí  /**\n   628‚Üí   * Handles input changes for simple input types (textarea, context)\n   629‚Üí   * \n   630‚Üí   * This function is used primarily for simple input types like textarea or context inputs.\n   631‚Üí   * Form inputs are handled separately by handleFormSubmit. When input changes, it updates\n   632‚Üí   * the stage state and marks the stage as requiring reprocessing.\n   633‚Üí   * \n   634‚Üí   * @param stageId - Unique identifier of the stage\n   635‚Üí   * @param fieldName - Name of the input field being changed\n   636‚Üí   * @param value - New value for the input field\n   637‚Üí   * \n   638‚Üí   * @example\n   639‚Üí   * ```typescript\n   640‚Üí   * handleInputChange('poem-topic', 'userInput', 'Write about nature');\n   641‚Üí   * ```\n   642‚Üí   */\n   643‚Üí  const handleInputChange = (stageId: string, fieldName: string, value: any) => {\n   644‚Üí    // This is primarily for simple input types like 'textarea' or 'context' now.\n   645‚Üí    // Form inputs are handled by onFormSubmit.\n   646‚Üí    if (fieldName === 'userInput') {\n   647‚Üí         updateStageState(stageId, { userInput: value, status: 'idle', output: undefined, completedAt: undefined, isStale: true });\n   648‚Üí    }\n   649‚Üí  };\n   650‚Üí\n   651‚Üí  /**\n   652‚Üí   * Handles form submissions and updates stage state accordingly\n   653‚Üí   * \n   654‚Üí   * This function is called when form field values change in the StageInputArea component.\n   655‚Üí   * It updates the central state with the latest form data and handles special cases for\n   656‚Üí   * form stages without prompt templates (which are immediately marked as completed).\n   657‚Üí   * \n   658‚Üí   * @param stageId - Unique identifier of the stage\n   659‚Üí   * @param data - Form data object containing all form field values\n   660‚Üí   * \n   661‚Üí   * Behavior:\n   662‚Üí   * - For form stages without promptTemplate: Immediately marks as completed with form data as output\n   663‚Üí   * - For other stages: Updates userInput and marks as requiring processing\n   664‚Üí   * - Triggers dependency evaluation and autorun for dependent stages\n   665‚Üí   * \n   666‚Üí   * @example\n   667‚Üí   * ```typescript\n   668‚Üí   * handleFormSubmit('audience-analysis', {\n   669‚Üí   *   targetAudience: 'Developers',\n   670‚Üí   *   contentType: 'Technical'\n   671‚Üí   * });\n   672‚Üí   * ```\n   673‚Üí   */\n   674‚Üí  const handleFormSubmit = (stageId: string, data: any) => {\n   675‚Üí    // This function is called from StageInputArea when form field values change.\n   676‚Üí    // It updates the central state with the latest form data.\n   677‚Üí    const stage = instance.workflow.stages.find(s => s.id === stageId);\n   678‚Üí    if (!stage) return;\n   679‚Üí\n   680‚Üí    // For form stages without a promptTemplate, immediately mark as completed with the form data as output\n   681‚Üí    if (stage.inputType === 'form' && !stage.promptTemplate) {\n   682‚Üí      updateStageState(stageId, { \n   683‚Üí        userInput: data,\n   684‚Üí        output: data, // Form data becomes the output\n   685‚Üí        status: 'completed',\n   686‚Üí        completedAt: new Date().toISOString(),\n   687‚Üí        isStale: false\n   688‚Üí      });\n   689‚Üí      // This will trigger dependency evaluation and autoRun stages will execute\n   690‚Üí    } else {\n   691‚Üí      // For other stages, just update the input\n   692‚Üí      updateStageState(stageId, { \n   693‚Üí        userInput: data, \n   694‚Üí        status: 'idle',\n   695‚Üí        isStale: true\n   696‚Üí      });\n   697‚Üí    }\n   698‚Üí  };\n   699‚Üí\n   700‚Üí  /**\n   701‚Üí   * Executes a workflow stage with comprehensive error handling and AI system integration\n   702‚Üí   * \n   703‚Üí   * This is the core stage execution function that handles both AI-powered stages and\n   704‚Üí   * non-AI stages (like export stages). It manages the complete execution lifecycle\n   705‚Üí   * including input validation, AI system readiness checks, error handling, and\n   706‚Üí   * state management.\n   707‚Üí   * \n   708‚Üí   * @param stageId - Unique identifier of the stage to execute\n   709‚Üí   * @param currentInput - Optional input data for the stage (overrides stage state)\n   710‚Üí   * @param aiRedoNotes - Optional notes for AI regeneration requests\n   711‚Üí   * @returns Promise that resolves when stage execution completes\n   712‚Üí   * \n   713‚Üí   * Stage execution process:\n   714‚Üí   * 1. **Pre-execution validation**: Checks AI system readiness and stage configuration\n   715‚Üí   * 2. **Input preparation**: Resolves template variables and prepares stage input\n   716‚Üí   * 3. **Execution routing**: Routes to appropriate handler (AI vs non-AI stages)\n   717‚Üí   * 4. **Result processing**: Validates and processes stage output\n   718‚Üí   * 5. **State management**: Updates stage state and triggers dependency evaluation\n   719‚Üí   * 6. **Error handling**: Comprehensive error catching and user feedback\n   720‚Üí   * \n   721‚Üí   * Special stage types:\n   722‚Üí   * - **AI stages**: Executed via AI stage runner with model-specific handling\n   723‚Üí   * - **Export stages**: Handled by specialized export stage execution\n   724‚Üí   * - **Form stages**: Process form data and trigger dependent stages\n   725‚Üí   * - **Template stages**: Resolve template variables from workflow context\n   726‚Üí   * \n   727‚Üí   * Error handling:\n   728‚Üí   * - AI system not ready errors with actionable solutions\n   729‚Üí   * - Template variable resolution errors with context information\n   730‚Üí   * - Network and API errors with retry suggestions\n   731‚Üí   * - Validation errors with clear user feedback\n   732‚Üí   * \n   733‚Üí   * @example\n   734‚Üí   * ```typescript\n   735‚Üí   * // Execute a stage with user input\n   736‚Üí   * await handleRunStage('poem-generation', userInput);\n   737‚Üí   * \n   738‚Üí   * // Execute with AI redo notes\n   739‚Üí   * await handleRunStage('poem-generation', undefined, 'Make it more romantic');\n   740‚Üí   * ```\n   741‚Üí   */\n   742‚Üí  const handleRunStage = useCallback(async (stageId: string, currentInput?: any, aiRedoNotes?: string) => {\n   743‚Üí    const stage = instance.workflow.stages.find(s => s.id === stageId);\n   744‚Üí    const stageTitle = stage?.title || stageId;\n   745‚Üí    const currentTime = Date.now();\n   746‚Üí    const timeSinceLoad = currentTime - aiLoadStartTime;\n   747‚Üí    \n   748‚Üí    console.log('[handleRunStage] AI readiness check:', {\n   749‚Üí      stageId,\n   750‚Üí      stageTitle,\n   751‚Üí      aiStageLoaded,\n   752‚Üí      runAiStageExists: !!runAiStage,\n   753‚Üí      aiLoadError,\n   754‚Üí      aiLoadAttempts,\n   755‚Üí      timeSinceLoadMs: timeSinceLoad,\n   756‚Üí      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),\n   757‚Üí    });\n   758‚Üí    \n   759‚Üí    if (!aiStageLoaded || !runAiStage) {\n   760‚Üí      const diagnosticInfo = {\n   761‚Üí        aiStageLoaded,\n   762‚Üí        runAiStageExists: !!runAiStage,\n   763‚Üí        aiLoadError,\n   764‚Üí        aiLoadAttempts,\n   765‚Üí        timeSinceLoadMs: timeSinceLoad,\n   766‚Üí        networkOnline: navigator.onLine,\n   767‚Üí        connectionType: (navigator as any).connection?.effectiveType || 'unknown',\n   768‚Üí        userAgent: navigator.userAgent,\n   769‚Üí        url: window.location.href,\n   770‚Üí        stageId,\n   771‚Üí        stageTitle,\n   772‚Üí      };\n   773‚Üí      \n   774‚Üí      console.error('[handleRunStage] üö® AI System Not Ready - Detailed Diagnostics:', diagnosticInfo);\n   775‚Üí      \n   776‚Üí      // Determine specific error cause and solution\n   777‚Üí      let errorTitle = \"AI System Not Ready\";\n   778‚Üí      let errorDescription = \"\";\n   779‚Üí      let actionableSteps: string[] = [];\n   780‚Üí      \n   781‚Üí      if (aiLoadError) {\n   782‚Üí        errorTitle = \"AI Module Failed to Load\";\n   783‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system encountered an error during initialization and cannot process \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   784‚Üí        actionableSteps = [\n   785‚Üí          \"Refresh the page to retry loading\",\n   786‚Üí          \"Check your internet connection\", \n   787‚Üí          \"Clear browser cache (Cmd/Ctrl + Shift + R)\",\n   788‚Üí          \"Check browser console for detailed error logs\",\n   789‚Üí          \"Contact support if the issue persists\"\n   790‚Üí        ];\n   791‚Üí      } else if (timeSinceLoad < 10000) {\n   792‚Üí        errorTitle = \"AI System Still Loading\";\n   793‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system is still initializing. Please wait a moment before running \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   794‚Üí        actionableSteps = [\n   795‚Üí          `Wait ${Math.ceil((10000 - timeSinceLoad) / 1000)} more seconds`,\n   796‚Üí          \"Try again in a few seconds\",\n   797‚Üí          \"Ensure stable internet connection\",\n   798‚Üí          \"Try refreshing if loading takes too long\"\n   799‚Üí        ];\n   800‚Üí      } else {\n   801‚Üí        errorTitle = \"AI System Load Timeout\";\n   802‚Üí        errorDescription = `The AI system failed to load after ${Math.round(timeSinceLoad / 1000)} seconds. Cannot process \"${stageTitle}\".`;\n   803‚Üí        actionableSteps = [\n   804‚Üí          \"Refresh the page (most likely to fix)\",\n   805‚Üí          \"Clear browser cache and cookies\",\n   806‚Üí          \"Check your internet connection speed\",\n   807‚Üí          \"Open browser console to see detailed errors\",\n   808‚Üí          \"Try a different browser or incognito mode\"\n   809‚Üí        ];\n   810‚Üí      }\n   811‚Üí      \n   812‚Üí      const detailedError = `${errorDescription}\n   813‚Üí\n   814‚ÜíTechnical Status:\n   815‚Üí‚Ä¢ AI Module Loaded: ${aiStageLoaded ? 'Yes' : 'No'}\n   816‚Üí‚Ä¢ Function Available: ${!!runAiStage ? 'Yes' : 'No'}\n   817‚Üí‚Ä¢ Load Attempts: ${aiLoadAttempts}/3\n   818‚Üí‚Ä¢ Time Since Page Load: ${Math.round(timeSinceLoad / 1000)}s\n   819‚Üí‚Ä¢ Network Status: ${navigator.onLine ? 'Online' : 'Offline'}\n   820‚Üí‚Ä¢ Connection: ${(navigator as any).connection?.effectiveType || 'Unknown'}\n   821‚Üí\n   822‚ÜíDeveloper Info:\n   823‚Üí‚Ä¢ Stage ID: ${stageId}\n   824‚Üí‚Ä¢ Stage Title: ${stageTitle}\n   825‚Üí‚Ä¢ Error: ${aiLoadError || 'No specific error'}\n   826‚Üí‚Ä¢ URL: ${window.location.href}\n   827‚Üí‚Ä¢ Timestamp: ${new Date().toISOString()}\n   828‚Üí\n   829‚ÜíSolutions (try in order):\n   830‚Üí${actionableSteps.map((step, i) => `${i + 1}. ${step}`).join('\\n')}\n   831‚Üí\n   832‚ÜíStill having issues? Check the browser console for detailed logs.`;\n   833‚Üí\n   834‚Üí      toast({\n   835‚Üí        title: errorTitle,\n   836‚Üí        description: detailedError,\n   837‚Üí        variant: \"destructive\",\n   838‚Üí        duration: 15000, // Show longer for complex troubleshooting\n   839‚Üí        action: (\n   840‚Üí          <Button\n   841‚Üí            onClick={() => {\n   842‚Üí              console.log('[handleRunStage] Manual retry requested from toast');\n   843‚Üí              setAiStageLoaded(false);\n   844‚Üí              setAiLoadError(null);\n   845‚Üí              setAiLoadAttempts(0);\n   846‚Üí              loadAiStageRunner();\n   847‚Üí            }}\n   848‚Üí            size=\"sm\"\n   849‚Üí          >\n   850‚Üí            Retry AI\n   851‚Üí          </Button>\n   852‚Üí        )\n   853‚Üí      });\n   854‚Üí      \n   855‚Üí      return;\n   856‚Üí    }\n   857‚Üí\n   858‚Üí    console.log('[handleRunStage] ‚úÖ AI system ready, proceeding with stage execution');\n   859‚Üí    console.log('[handleRunStage] Called with:', { stageId, currentInput, hasAiRedoNotes: !!aiRedoNotes });\n   860‚Üí    if (!stage) return;\n   861‚Üí\n   862‚Üí
